        9 = IMPERATORI_CONSORT
	}
	
	consort_female = {
		6 = BATONISHVILI_CONSORT_fem
		7 = BATONISHVILI_CONSORT_fem
        8 = BATONISHVILI_CONSORT_fem
        9 = DEDOPALI_CONSORT_fem
	}

	heir_male = {
		6 = BATONISHVILI
		7 = BATONISHVILI
		8 = BATONISHVILI
		9 = BATONISHVILI
	}

	heir_female = {
		6 = BATONISHVILI_fem
		7 = BATONISHVILI_fem
		8 = BATONISHVILI_fem
		9 = BATONISHVILI_fem
	}

    trigger = {
	    government = monarchy
		AND = {
			OR = {

		    }

			}
		}

    }
}
